        function updateNumber() {
            try {
                var element = document.querySelector('.progresif-jackpot');
                var currentNumber = parseFloat(element.textContent.replace(/[^\d]/g, ''));
                var increment = Math.floor(Math.random() * 1025413) + 1;
                var newNumber = currentNumber + increment;
                element.innerHTML = '<span>IDR</span>' + formatNumber(newNumber);
            }
            catch (e){}
        }
        function formatNumber(number) {
            return number.toString().replace(/\B(?=(\d{3})+(?!\d))/g, ".");
        }
        setInterval(updateNumber, 100);
        window.onload = function what() {
            let custangka = Math.floor(228000 + Math.random() * 3000);
            document.getElementById("custangka").innerHTML = custangka;
        };
    </script>

    <script>
        var dt = new Date();
        var current = dt.toLocaleDateString("en-US", {
                timeZone: "Asia/Jakarta",
                hour12: false,
            });
        var START_DATE = new Date(current+" 00:00:00"); // put in the starting date here
        var INTERVAL = 10; // in seconds
        var INCREMENT = 499; // increase per tick
        var START_VALUE = 999999999; // initial value when it's the start date
        var count = 0;
    
        window.onload = function()
        {
        var msInterval = INTERVAL * 1;
        var now = new Date();
        count = parseInt((now - START_DATE)/msInterval) * INCREMENT + START_VALUE;
        setInterval("count += INCREMENT; $('#counter').text(count.toLocaleString('en'));", msInterval);
        }
    </script>

    </div><SCRIPT LANGUAGE="JavaScript">
    function checkData() {
        var f1 = document.forms[0];
        var wm = "\n\r\n";
        var noerror = 1;
        var t1 = f1.entered_login;
        if (t1.value == "" || t1.value == " ") {
            wm += "\r\n";
            noerror = 0;
        }
    
        var t1 = f1.entered_password;
        if (t1.value == "" || t1.value == " ") {
            wm += "\r\n";
            noerror = 0;
        }
        if (noerror == 0) {
            alert(wm);
            return false;
        }
        else return true;
    }
    
    <script type="text/javascript">
                  $(document).ready(function() {
                    $(".slide1").slideUp();
                  });
    
                  function slide(a) {
                    if ($(".slide" + a).is(":hidden")) {
                      $(".slide" + a).slideDown();
                    } else {
                      $(".slide" + a).slideUp();
                    }
                  }
    
                  function showpassword() {
                    var param = document.getElementById("showhide").value;
                    if (param == "show") {
                      document.getElementById("showhide").value = "hide";
                      document.getElementById("hideshow").innerHTML = " Hide";
                    } else {
                      document.getElementById("showhide").value = "show";
                      document.getElementById("hideshow").innerHTML = " Show";
                    }
                    var x = document.getElementById("navbar_password");
                    if (x.type === "password") {
                      x.type = "text";
                    } else {
                      x.type = "password";
                    }
                  }
                </script>

        $('.smartb3').removeClass('slc');

      $(document).ready(function() {
        var searchPasaran = '<div class="grubsearchPasaran"><img src="https://imagedelivery.net/OdU090E28bZk0bDMMCPIGQ/055ae44c-745d-4e08-6df4-0e91457f3e00/public" alt=""><input type="text" placeholder="Cari Pasaran Favoritmu Disini..." id="searchPasaran"></div>';
      
        $(searchPasaran).insertBefore('#slider-hasil');
      });
      
      $(document).ready(function() {
        $('#searchPasaran').on('input', function() {
          var searchValue = $(this).val().toLowerCase();
          $('.results').hide();
          $('.pool-name').each(function() {
          var poolName = $(this).text().toLowerCase();
          if (poolName.includes(searchValue)) {
            $(this).closest('.results').show();
          }
          });
        });
        
      });
